## Validation Test Lifecycle Governance (2026-04-30)
- status: queued
- rollup_refresh_required: true
- policy_ref: validation/tests/README.md
- purpose: move tests, gates, evals, benchmarks, conformance checks, and release checks from ad hoc scaffolding into a governed lifecycle with owner, invariant, evidence, strengthening signal, and exit criteria.
- [x] TEST-LIFE-001 Create a canonical Validation-owned test lifecycle registry and retire the old test maturity registry compatibility mirror. Evidence: `validation/tests/contracts/validation_test_lifecycle_registry.json` now owns the lifecycle registry, `validation/tests/compatibility_mirrors.json` records the mirror as retired, and `tests/tooling/scripts/ci/test_maturity_registry_guard.ts` defaults to the Validation path while failing closed if the retired tooling mirror is reintroduced.
- [x] TEST-LIFE-002 Add suite-level lifecycle manifests so individual test suites declare `classification`, `owner`, `runtime_owner`, `invariant`, `evidence_artifact`, `lifecycle_state`, and whether they are temporary. Evidence: `validation/tests/contracts/test_suite_lifecycle_manifests.json` now declares suite-level lifecycle metadata for the test maturity registry, Assurance physical-domain gates, eval feedback lifecycle, Shell projection ownership, Kernel Sentinel release observation, and issue-candidate actionability. `tests/tooling/scripts/ci/test_maturity_registry_guard.ts` now validates the suite manifest path, required fields, lifecycle states, classifications, temporary flags, and managed-gate classification coverage.
- [x] TEST-LIFE-003 Standardize lifecycle artifact envelopes so every managed test emits `ok`, `test_id`, `classification`, `invariant`, `runtime_owner`, `failure_signature`, and `strengthen_signal`. Evidence: `validation/tests/contracts/test_lifecycle_artifact_envelope_contract.json` defines the canonical envelope contract. `tests/tooling/scripts/ci/test_maturity_registry_guard.ts` now validates that contract and emits `lifecycle_artifact_envelopes` for every managed registry entry, including normalized runtime owner, invariant, strengthening signal, and stable failure signatures for unhealthy lifecycle rows.
- [x] TEST-LIFE-004 Expand temporary test contracts to every scaffold/monitor/crutch, requiring `why_it_exists`, runtime weakness signal, minimum runs, success rate, expiry, migration target, and delete-or-merge condition. Evidence: `validation/tests/contracts/temporary_test_lifecycle_contract.json` now defines the temporary lifecycle contract. Existing temporary monitor rows in `validation/tests/contracts/validation_test_lifecycle_registry.json` and the compatibility mirror now carry unified `why_it_exists`, `runtime_weakness_signal`, and numeric success criteria. `tests/tooling/scripts/ci/test_maturity_registry_guard.ts` fails closed when any temporary scaffold, monitor, runtime crutch, or one-time closure guard omits required fields or success criteria.
- [x] TEST-LIFE-005 Extend retirement backlog automation so met success criteria create operator-reviewable retire/merge backlog items instead of relying on manual cleanup. Evidence: `tests/tooling/scripts/ci/test_maturity_registry_guard.ts` now emits structured `retirement_action_items` into `core/local/artifacts/test_maturity_retirement_backlog_current.json` whenever temporary monitor success criteria are met. Each action declares review-required/no-auto-delete policy, runtime owner, migration target, delete condition, observed run window, and validation commands for the retire/merge cleanup path.
- [x] TEST-LIFE-006 Add runtime-strengthening feedback aggregation that maps recurring test failures or expired monitors to the subsystem that needs stronger runtime self-enforcement. Evidence: `tests/tooling/scripts/ci/test_maturity_registry_guard.ts` now emits `runtime_strengthening_feedback` in `core/local/artifacts/test_maturity_registry_current.json` and the operator markdown report. The feedback groups unhealthy lifecycle envelopes, blocked temporary monitors, and non-info findings by runtime owner with affected gates, failure signatures, strengthening signals, and a recommended runtime self-enforcement action.
- [x] TEST-LIFE-007 Enforce physical Validation placement for test/eval/benchmark/conformance/release definitions while keeping `tests/tooling/**` as harness-only execution infrastructure. Evidence: `validation/tests/contracts/test_lifecycle_physical_placement_policy.json` now defines canonical Validation definition prefixes, harness-only tooling prefixes, forbidden tooling-definition prefixes, and the required compatibility mirror. `tests/tooling/scripts/ci/test_maturity_registry_guard.ts` validates that lifecycle registry, suite manifest, artifact envelope contract, temporary-test contract, and placement policy live under `validation/**`; validates suite owners are Validation-domain owners; and verifies the gate command reads Validation-owned definitions while keeping the old tooling registry explicit as a compatibility mirror.
- [x] TEST-LIFE-008 Add an unregistered-test guard so new tests/gates/suites fail governance unless registered, declared `harness_only`, or explicitly exempted with owner and expiry. Evidence: `validation/tests/contracts/unregistered_test_policy.json` now defines the registration policy. `tests/tooling/scripts/ci/test_maturity_registry_guard.ts` now validates that every tooling gate is lifecycle-registered, declared harness-only, or covered by an owner/reason/expiry exemption; rejects expired or malformed exemptions; and reports unregistered gate counts in the lifecycle artifact.

## Kernel Sentinel Architectural Synthesis Upgrade (2026-04-29)
- status: queued
- rollup_refresh_required: true
- policy_ref: docs/workspace/system_understanding_dossier_policy.md
- purpose: upgrade Sentinel from artifact health collector into a multilevel architectural observer that can recognize source-of-truth, policy, and self-model failures before remediation drifts into symptom patching.
- [x] KSA-SYN-001 Add a required Sentinel failure-level taxonomy: `L0_local_defect`, `L1_component_regression`, `L2_boundary_contract_breach`, `L3_policy_truth_failure`, `L4_architectural_misalignment`, and `L5_self_model_failure`. Evidence: `core/layer0/ops/src/kernel_sentinel/failure_level.rs` defines the stable taxonomy, `core/layer0/ops/src/kernel_sentinel/authority.rs` exposes it in the Kernel Sentinel contract, `core/layer0/ops/src/kernel_sentinel/root_tests.rs` covers contract exposure, and `docs/workspace/SRS.md` tracks `V13-KSENT-SYN-001`.
- [x] KSA-SYN-002 Require every Sentinel finding, feedback item, and issue candidate to carry `failure_level`, `root_frame`, and `remediation_level` fields. Evidence: `KernelSentinelFinding` now serializes semantic frame fields, and Sentinel issue drafts, maintenance suggestions, automation candidates, self-study feedback items, top-hole issue candidates, and RSI readiness issue candidates now carry `failure_level`, `root_frame`, and `remediation_level`. Validation: targeted `cargo test --manifest-path core/layer0/ops/Cargo.toml <filter> -- --nocapture` loop passed for finding schema, issue synthesis, maintenance synthesis, self-study feedback, top-hole issue candidates, and auto-run RSI readiness candidates.

## Tauri Desktop App Migration + Memory Fix Wave (2026-04-27)

Queued: 24 items. Intent: migrate from browser dashboard → Tauri desktop app, fix unbounded memory growth, and align UI with OS shell pattern.

|----|--------|----------|-------|
| Tauri-UI-001 | queued | 10 | Add UI Projection Layer — stop sending full orchestration payloads to UI |
| Tauri-UI-002 | queued | 10 | Cap In-Memory Chat — keep only last N messages in UI state |
| Tauri-UI-003 | queued | 10 | Remove Default Decision Trace Rendering — lazy-load behind expand |
| Tauri-UI-004 | queued | 10 | Create Data Access Layer (DAL) — backend API for paginated chat data |
| Tauri-UI-005 | queued | 10 | Introduce Chat Storage (SQLite) — persist messages off-memory |
| Tauri-UI-006 | queued | 10 | Add Windowed Loading — virtualization backed by storage |
| Tauri-UI-007 | queued | 10 | Replace Snapshot State with Streaming — incremental UI updates |
| Tauri-UI-008 | queued | 10 | Add Event Bus (Backend) — pub/sub for MessageAdded/Updated/ExecutionUpdate |
| Tauri-UI-009 | queued | 10 | Deduplicate Subscriptions — prevent memory leaks from duplicate listeners |
| Tauri-UI-010 | queued | 10 | Scaffold Tauri App — replace browser runtime with local executable |
| Tauri-UI-011 | queued | 10 | Build IPC Layer — commands and events replacing HTTP/WebSocket |
| Tauri-UI-012 | queued | 10 | Connect to Infring Core — direct Rust runtime integration over IPC |
| Tauri-UI-013 | queued | 10 | Add Message Detail Lazy Loading — decision trace/signals on demand |
| Tauri-UI-014 | queued | 10 | Compress Old Messages — summarization for long-session storage |
| Tauri-UI-015 | queued | 10 | Add Memory Metrics — track RAM, message count, render time |
| Tauri-UI-016 | queued | 9 | Treat UI as Shell — enforce no logic, no core calls from UI |
| Tauri-UI-017 | queued | 9 | Introduce Session Kernel Interface — formal InfringKernel trait boundary |
| Tauri-UI-018 | queued | 9 | Add Offline Capability — cache sessions, run without network |

## Chat Dashboard Alpine → Svelte Migration Wave (2026-04-27)

Queued: 18 items. Intent: eliminate Alpine.js reactive proxy overhead from the chat dashboard, which accounts for the ~750MB "system" JS heap from Alpine wrapping every property of every message object and all chat state. Items are ordered by dependency — each step is independently shippable. The Svelte custom element shells (`chat_page_shell`, `chat_thread_shell`, `chat_input_footer_shell`, etc.) already exist as stubs and are the migration targets.

| ID | Status | Priority | Title |
|----|--------|----------|-------|
| SVELTE-001 | done | 9 | Define `chatStore.ts` — create Svelte writable stores for `messages`, `currentAgent`, `sessionLoading`, `sending`; no behavioral change, just the target store definitions |
| SVELTE-002 | done | 9 | Move `messages[]` from Alpine to Svelte store — update all write sites in `chat.ts` to call `messagesStore.set()`; Alpine reads via a thin `$messages` adapter so nothing else breaks |
| SVELTE-003 | done | 9 | Move streaming/thinking rows to Svelte store — WS handlers (`150-ws-stream-handlers.ts`) write to the store instead of `this.messages`; `clearTransientThinkingRows` updates the store |
| SVELTE-004 | done | 9 | Replace `x-for` message loop with Svelte `{#each}` in `chat_thread_shell` — message rendering driven directly by the Svelte store; this eliminates Alpine's proxy over the entire messages array |
| SVELTE-005 | done | 8 | Move `sending`, `chatInputText`, `tokenCount` to Svelte store — scoped to the send pipeline (`200-send-pipeline.part01.ts`); Alpine reads via adapter |
| SVELTE-006 | done | 8 | Replace Alpine input binding with `chat_input_footer_shell` Svelte component — the stub already exists; wire it to `chatStore` for two-way input binding and send dispatch |
| SVELTE-007 | done | 8 | Move `currentAgent`, `agents[]`, `sessionLoading`, `_sessionLoadSeq` to Svelte store — `loadSession` and `loadOlderMessages` write to the store |
| SVELTE-008 | done | 8 | Replace agent sidebar Alpine loop with Svelte component — agent list rendered via Svelte store; enables granular per-agent reactivity instead of full-list re-evaluation |
| SVELTE-009 | done | 7 | Move WS connection lifecycle to a Svelte-native module — `wsConnect`/`wsDisconnect` and event dispatch decoupled from the Alpine component object; event handlers call store setters directly |
| SVELTE-010 | done | 7 | Move scroll and viewport state (`_stickToBottom`, `showScrollDown`, `mapStepIndex`) to Svelte store — decouples scroll logic from Alpine reactivity cycle |
| SVELTE-011 | done | 6 | Replace `Alpine.store('app')` with Svelte context — global app state (model catalog, feature flags, global agent list) provided via `setContext`/`getContext` from `chat_page_shell` |
| SVELTE-012 | queued | 6 | Remove `x-data="chatPage"` root binding from HTML — replace `chat-wrapper` div with `<infring-chat-page-shell>` as the Svelte root; delete `chatPage()` function from `chat.ts` |
| SVELTE-013 | queued | 5 | Remove Alpine from the bundle — delete Alpine import from `app.ts`, remove from `package.json`; verify no remaining `x-data`/`x-bind`/`x-on` in HTML templates |
| SVELTE-014 | queued | 9 | Make `InfringChatStore` the single owner of live message state — route streaming/thinking/tool/result mutation through store-backed helpers so message rows are not co-owned reactively by Alpine and Svelte |
| SVELTE-015 | queued | 8 | Remove Alpine per-message UI ownership — move hover, expanded tool-card state, metadata-collapse state, and other row-local view state into the Svelte thread layer |
| SVELTE-016 | queued | 10 | Add real long-chat windowing with cheap offscreen placeholders — keep full bubble rendering only inside a bounded visible range and replace offscreen history with low-cost shells to bound RAM and DOM growth |
| SVELTE-017 | queued | 8 | Reduce retained per-message payload weight — compact or defer rich tool outputs, workspace artifacts, rendered HTML, source-chip payloads, and thought/tool traces so long sessions do not retain full heavy envelopes in memory |
| SVELTE-018 | queued | 7 | Add shell chat memory profiling and regression evidence — capture heap size, DOM node count, retained message object count, and scroll performance by message volume so RAM-reduction waves can be measured and gated |

## Shell Alpine Purge Wave (2026-04-28)

Remaining queued: 0 of 14 items. Intent: remove Alpine.js from active shell runtime in controlled waves after the Misty long-chat memory regression showed that one remaining `x-for` over `messages` can defeat Svelte projection and push the browser heap into multi-GB territory. The migration rule is strict: Svelte owns rendering/local interaction state, shared shell services own reusable mechanics, and core/orchestration keep authority. Alpine may remain only as temporary glue until each owner is replaced.

| ID | Status | Priority | Title |
|----|--------|----------|-------|
| ALPINE-PURGE-001 | done | 10 | Freeze new Alpine usage — `ops:shell:alpine-growth:guard` now reports and strict-fails growth for `x-data`, `x-for`, `x-model`, `x-bind`, `x-on`, direct `Alpine.store`, broad `x-*`, shorthand events/bindings, and Alpine magic helpers |
| ALPINE-PURGE-002 | done | 10 | Add hot-path Alpine fail guard — `ops:shell:alpine-hot-path:guard` now hard-fails active `x-for` over `messages`, `filteredMessages`, `agents`, `sessions`, chat map rows, chat sidebar rows, and other unbounded shell collections; current live shell correctly fails closed on remaining hot-path debt |
| ALPINE-PURGE-003 | done | 10 | Make chat thread Svelte canonical — removed the legacy Alpine message renderer from the main chat page, verified the main chat and inline agent chat both mount `<infring-chat-thread-shell>`, and updated the chat rendering guard to fail if the retired renderer returns |
| ALPINE-PURGE-004 | done | 10 | Move chat map rendering to Svelte — replaced the active Alpine chat-map message loop with a Svelte-owned renderer backed by lightweight `mapRows` projection data; live hot-path debt dropped from 9 active loops to 8 |
| ALPINE-PURGE-005 | done | 10 | Move chat sidebar rendering to Svelte — replaced the active Alpine sidebar visible-row loop with `infring-sidebar-agent-list-shell`, keeping shared dragbar parent mechanics while delegating row selection, archive, popup, and topology drag/drop actions back to existing shell methods; live hot-path debt dropped from 8 active loops to 7 |
| ALPINE-PURGE-006 | done | 9 | Move chat input/composer ownership fully to Svelte — replaced the active main and inline Alpine composer surfaces with `infring-chat-input-footer-shell`, preserving existing shell action delegates for text/terminal mode, hamburger menu, attachments, git/model menus, prompt suggestions, queued prompts, send/stop, and voice controls; composer Alpine binding tokens are now guarded absent from active chat body parts |
| ALPINE-PURGE-007 | done | 9 | Move popups/dropdowns/menu positioning to shared shell services plus Svelte callers — removed active dashboard popup overlay rendering from Alpine popup-origin helpers, moved taskbar menu orientation class application into `infring-taskbar-menu-shell`, and added popup runtime guard checks that fail if active markup calls the retired Alpine rendering helpers again |
| ALPINE-PURGE-008 | done | 9 | Move taskbar/dock rendering and interaction state to Svelte — replaced the active bottom dock and right taskbar system item Alpine markup with `infring-bottom-dock-shell` and `infring-taskbar-system-items-shell`, preserving shared taskbar/dock and dragbar delegates while removing the active dock tile and notification/taskbar item loops from Alpine-owned HTML |
| ALPINE-PURGE-009 | done | 8 | Move agent details drawer to Svelte — active chat HTML now mounts an empty `infring-agent-details-shell`; the Svelte island owns tabs, permissions, identity editing, avatar controls, fallbacks, and save flow while delegating unchanged backend/page contracts through `window.InfringChatPage` |
| ALPINE-PURGE-010 | done | 8 | Move remaining page panels to Svelte shells — expanded simple-page-panel Svelte ownership from the first overview/agents/settings/workflows slice to all remaining route page shells and their tab panels, including scheduler, channels, eyes, skills, hands, analytics, sessions, logs, comms, wizard, and runtime |
| ALPINE-PURGE-011 | done | 8 | Replace `Alpine.store('app')` with a shell app store bridge — added `InfringSharedShellServices.appStore`, moved app-store bootstrap through the bridge, registered the shell root for route/page/theme/agent snapshots, migrated active Svelte app-store callers to the bridge, and added `ops:shell:app-store-bridge:guard` coverage |
| ALPINE-PURGE-012 | blocked | 7 | Remove Alpine boot path — blocked until `ops:shell:alpine-retirement:guard` and `ops:shell:alpine-hot-path:guard` are green; current proof shows live Alpine bindings/API reads remain, including 7 active hot-path loops and the router's `vendor/alpine.min` loader |
| ALPINE-PURGE-013 | done | 8 | Add RAM regression gate for long chats — added `ops:shell:long-chat-ram:guard`, which validates the live `/memprobe` heap/DOM/custom-element contract, executes `InfringChatStore` against a 1,000-message synthetic thread, records before/after heap and DOM budget snapshots, and fails if projected Svelte thread rows, heavy bubble instances, estimated heap growth, or DOM counts become unbounded |
| ALPINE-PURGE-014 | blocked | 7 | Delete Alpine vendor/runtime artifact — blocked because Alpine is still an active shell dependency: `ops:shell:alpine-retirement:guard` reports 3456 live Alpine hits plus the router's `vendor/alpine.min` loader, and `ops:shell:alpine-hot-path:guard` reports 7 active hot-path Alpine loops; deleting `vendor/alpine.min.ts` now would break the live dashboard |
